	local captainsSlain = Hydra.QuestCallbackCountGet(622)
	local flAutoOpenTime = 8
	
	Hydra.Wait(1)
	
	if captainsSlain >= 1 then
		
		Hydra.QuestSpawnRewardChest(ACTOR_CHEST_REWARD_TIER1, ID_CHEST_SPAWN_LOC_2, flAutoOpenTime)
		
	end
	
	if captainsSlain >= 2 then
		Hydra.Wait(1)
		Hydra.QuestSpawnRewardChest(ACTOR_CHEST_REWARD_TIER2, ID_CHEST_SPAWN_LOC_3, flAutoOpenTime)
	end
	
	if captainsSlain >= 3 then
		Hydra.Wait(1)
		if bBossKilled then
			Hydra.QuestSpawnRewardChest(ACTOR_CHEST_REWARD_TIER4, ID_CHEST_SPAWN_LOC, flAutoOpenTime)
		else
			Hydra.QuestSpawnRewardChest(ACTOR_CHEST_REWARD_TIER3, ID_CHEST_SPAWN_LOC, flAutoOpenTime)
		end
	end

	Hydra.EventSend("EnableCampfire")
	Hydra.SetGameVariableFlag("ZE_SpawnerDelay")
	Hydra.ClearWeatherOverride(strWorld)
end

	for i=1, #tIntroCaptains do
		Hydra.ActorEnableAI(tIntroCaptains[i], false)
		Hydra.ActorSetTargetable(tIntroCaptains[i], false)
		Hydra.ActorTriggerPowerAtFeet(tIntroCaptains[i], ChannelPower)
		Hydra.BuffApplyToTarget(ZEBuffPower, "SHADOW_SHADER_BUFF", tIntroCaptains[i])
		Hydra.ActorEnable(tIntroCaptains[i])
		Hydra.ActorPlayEffectGroupActorToActor(tIntroCaptains[i], introSummonLoc, IntroTetherFX, true, "HP_center")
	end
	Hydra.ActorSetPowerEffectSize(introSummonLoc, 7)
	Hydra.ActorPlayEffectGroup(introSummonLoc, IntroSpawningFX, true)
	
	--apply buff to base pop monsters so they despawn if out of combat
	for i, idActor in pairs(Hydra.ActorsInGroup("ZE_BasePop")) do
		Hydra.ActorTriggerPowerAtFeet(idActor, CombatDespawnPower)
	end

</td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_47705e2</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>arLevelAreas</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>arSubzones</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>arSnonameTokens</b></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_5342cc0</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>dwFlags</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>unk_9c1ea4f</b></td><td><code>0</code></td></tr><tr><td><b>szOnCallbackCompleteScript</b></td><td><pre>function Start()
	Hydra.QuestCallbackCountSet(618, Hydra.QuestCallbackCountGet(622))
	nTier = Hydra.QuestCallbackCountGet(618)
	Hydra.BuffApplyToTarget(POWER_DROP_NO_LOOT, "MAIN", mainBoss)
	
	Hydra.Wait(1)
	--Spawn end boss based on tier reached
	if nTier == 0 then
	elseif nTier == 1 then
		Hydra.ActorEnableAI(mainBoss, true)
		Hydra.ActorPlayEffectGroup(idFXMarker, BarrierExplodeFX)
		Hydra.BuffRemove(ZEBuffPower, "SHADOW_SHADER_BUFF", mainBoss)
		Hydra.ActorDelete(bossBarrier)
		Hydra.ActorSetTargetable(mainBoss, true)
		Hydra.ActorMergeAIState(mainBoss, AI_BossLeash, mainBoss)
	elseif nTier == 2 then
		Hydra.QActorAnim(mainBoss, Power_Boss_Summon)
		Hydra.Wait(1.5)
		Hydra.ActorTriggerSpawnerUpdateLinkedToActor(ID_THIS_QUEST, "BossT3")
		Hydra.Wait(1.5)
		Hydra.ActorEnableAI(mainBoss, true)
		Hydra.ActorPlayEffectGroup(idFXMarker, BarrierExplodeFX)
		Hydra.BuffRemove(ZEBuffPower, "SHADOW_SHADER_BUFF", mainBoss)
		Hydra.ActorDelete(bossBarrier)
		Hydra.ActorSetTargetable(mainBoss, true)
		Hydra.ActorMergeAIState(mainBoss, AI_BossLeash, mainBoss)
	elseif nTier == 3 then
		Hydra.QActorAnim(mainBoss, Power_Boss_Summon)
		Hydra.Wait(1.5)
		Hydra.ActorTriggerSpawnerUpdateLinkedToActor(ID_THIS_QUEST, "BossT1")
		Hydra.ActorTriggerSpawnerUpdateLinkedToActor(ID_THIS_QUEST, "BossT3")
		Hydra.Wait(1.5)
		Hydra.ActorEnableAI(mainBoss, true)
		Hydra.ActorPlayEffectGroup(idFXMarker, BarrierExplodeFX)
		Hydra.BuffRemove(ZEBuffPower, "SHADOW_SHADER_BUFF", mainBoss)
		Hydra.ActorDelete(bossBarrier)
		Hydra.ActorSetTargetable(mainBoss, true)
		Hydra.ActorMergeAIState(mainBoss, AI_BossLeash, mainBoss)
		
	end
	
	--remove vfx
	if nTier > 1 then
		Hydra.ActorRemoveComplexEffect(BossLoc, BossSpawnFX)
	end
end

		local nCurrentProgress = Hydra.QuestCallbackCountGet(836)
		Hydra.QuestCallbackCountSet(836, nCurrentProgress + nFakeProgress)
	end
end
</pre></td></tr></table>

</td></tr><tr><td><b>szOnCallbackCompleteScript</b></td><td><pre>function Start()
	
	
	
	bEventStarted = true
	-- Override weather
	if (strLevelArea == S_ZONE_NAME_FRAC) then
		Hydra.WeatherOverride(strWorld, S_WEATHER_INVASION_FRAC);
	elseif (strLevelArea == S_ZONE_NAME_HAWE) then
		Hydra.WeatherOverride(strWorld, S_WEATHER_INVASION_HAWE);
	elseif (strLevelArea == S_CAMP_NAME_HAWE) then
		bHaweCamp = true;
	elseif (strLevelArea == S_ZONE_NAME_KEHJ) then
		Hydra.WeatherOverride(strWorld, S_WEATHER_INVASION_KEHJ);
	elseif (strLevelArea == S_CAMP_NAME_KEHJ) then
		bKehjCamp = true;
	elseif (strLevelArea == S_ZONE_NAME_SCOS) then
		Hydra.WeatherOverride(strWorld, S_WEATHER_INVASION_SCOS);
	elseif (strLevelArea == S_ZONE_NAME_STEP or strLevelArea == S_CAMP_NAME_STEP) then
		Hydra.WeatherOverride(strWorld, S_WEATHER_INVASION_STEP);
	else
		Hydra.WeatherOverride(strWorld, S_WEATHER_INVASION_DEFAULT);
	end
	
	
	Hydra.EventSend("DisableCampfire")
	
	
	Hydra.Wait(1)
	for i=1, #tIntroCaptains do
		Hydra.BuffApplyToTarget(ZEBuffPower, "FADEOUT_BUFF_NOTIMER", tIntroCaptains[i])
	end
	Hydra.ActorRemoveComplexEffectByEffectGroupSNO(introSummonLoc, IntroSpawningFX)
	Hydra.ActorSetPowerEffectSize(introSummonLoc, 15)
	Hydra.ActorPlayEffectGroup(introSummonLoc, BarrierExplodeFX)
	Hydra.Wait(.5)
	--have boss appear
	introBoss = Hydra.ActorsLinkedByActorInGroup(ID_THIS_QUEST, "introBoss")[1]
	bossBarrier = Hydra.ActorsLinkedByActorInGroup(ID_THIS_QUEST, "bossBarrier")[1]
	Hydra.BuffApplyToTarget(ZEBuffPower, "SHADOW_SHADER_BUFF", introBoss)
	Hydra.ActorTriggerPowerAtTarget(introBoss, introSummonLoc, Power_Boss_Intro, true)
	Hydra.Wait(1)
	Hydra.QActorAnim(introBoss, Power_Boss_Summon)
	Hydra.DisplayGameMessageForAllQuestParticipants("Messages:ZE_GatheringHorde_BossIntro")
	
	--hard cleanup on ambient monsters in the space
	for i, idActor in pairs(Hydra.ActorsInGroup("ZE_BasePop")) do
		Hydra.BuffApplyToTarget(ZEBuffPower, "SHADOW_SHADER_MINION_BUFF", idActor)
	end
	
end

		Hydra.EventSendToActor("STOP_EVENT", ID_THIS_QUEST, idActor)

	Hydra.ActorSetPowerEffectSize(BossLoc, 10)
	if nTier > 1 then
		BossSpawnFX = Hydra.ActorPlayEffectGroup(BossLoc, Boss_LocFX, true)
	end
	--have the skeleton boss in a barrier

	--spawn a marker loc so burst fx can be played on it when deleting the barrier
	idFXMarker = Hydra.ActorSpawnActor(ACTOR_MARKERLOCATION, bossBarrier, false, 0, 0)
	Hydra.ActorSetPowerEffectSize(idFXMarker, 20)

local function advanceTier()

	Hydra.EventSend("TIER_COMPLETE")
	nCurrentTier = nCurrentTier + 1
	
end
